Rule Scheduler (schedule/schedule.go)**\\n- `Run()` (line 175): Main entry point that starts the scheduler with a ticker\\n- `schedulePeriodic()` (line 246): Main scheduler loop that processes ticks at the configured base interval\\n- `processTick()` (line 276): Called on each tick, determines which rules are ready to run based on their evaluation intervals, creates rule routines, and schedules evaluations\\n- `runJobFn()` (line 426): Called to schedule individual rule evaluations with optional jitter, sends evaluation signals to rule routines\\n\\n**2.
